    <script type="text/javascript">
        document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
            function autoHideMessage(elementId, delay) {
                const messageElement = document.getElementById(elementId);
                if (messageElement && messageElement.classList.contains('show')) {
                    setTimeout(function() {
                        var alertInstance = bootstrap.Alert.getInstance(messageElement);
                        if (alertInstance) {
                            alertInstance.close();
                        } else {
                            messageElement.style.transition = 'opacity 0.5s ease-out';
                            messageElement.style.opacity = '0';
                            setTimeout(() => { messageElement.style.display = 'none'; }, 500);
                        }
                    }, delay);
                } else if (messageElement) { 
                     setTimeout(function() {
                        messageElement.style.transition = 'opacity 0.5s ease-out';
                        messageElement.style.opacity = '0';
                        setTimeout(() => { messageElement.style.display = 'none'; }, 500);
                    }, delay);
                }
            }
            autoHideMessage('flashAdvancedOrderError', 7000); 
        });
    </script>
</body>

        document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
            function autoHideMessage(elementId, delay) {
                const messageElement = document.getElementById(elementId);
                if (messageElement && messageElement.classList.contains('show')) {
                    setTimeout(function() {
                        var alertInstance = bootstrap.Alert.getInstance(messageElement);
                        if (alertInstance) {
                            alertInstance.close();
                        } else {
                            messageElement.style.display = 'none';
                        }
                    }, delay);
                }
            }

            autoHideMessage('flashErrorMessage', 7000);  // Error messages hide after 7 seconds
        });

    <script type="text/javascript">
        document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
            function autoHideMessage(elementId, delay) {
                const messageElement = document.getElementById(elementId);
                if (messageElement && messageElement.classList.contains('show')) { // Check if it's a Bootstrap alert still visible
                    setTimeout(function() {
                        var alertInstance = bootstrap.Alert.getInstance(messageElement);
                        if (alertInstance) {
                            alertInstance.close();
                        } else {
                             // Fallback for non-Bootstrap elements or if getInstance fails
                            messageElement.style.transition = 'opacity 0.5s ease-out';
                            messageElement.style.opacity = '0';
                            setTimeout(() => { messageElement.style.display = 'none'; }, 500);
                        }
                    }, delay);
                } else if (messageElement) { // For non-Bootstrap alert elements that don't have 'show'
                     setTimeout(function() {
                        messageElement.style.transition = 'opacity 0.5s ease-out';
                        messageElement.style.opacity = '0';
                        setTimeout(() => { messageElement.style.display = 'none'; }, 500);
                    }, delay);
                }
            }
            autoHideMessage('flashLoginSuccessMessage', 5000); 
            autoHideMessage('flashLoginErrorMessage', 7000);
            autoHideMessage('flashRedirectMessage', 7000); // For messages from AuthenticationFilter redirect
        });
    </script>
</body>
</html>

    <script type="text/javascript">
        document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
            function autoHideMessage(elementId, delay) {
                const messageElement = document.getElementById(elementId);
                if (messageElement && messageElement.classList.contains('show')) {
                    setTimeout(function() {
                        var alertInstance = bootstrap.Alert.getInstance(messageElement);
                        if (alertInstance) {
                            alertInstance.close();
                        } else {
                            messageElement.style.transition = 'opacity 0.5s ease-out';
                            messageElement.style.opacity = '0';
                            setTimeout(() => { messageElement.style.display = 'none'; }, 500);
                        }
                    }, delay);
                } else if (messageElement) { 
                     setTimeout(function() {
                        messageElement.style.transition = 'opacity 0.5s ease-out';
                        messageElement.style.opacity = '0';
                        setTimeout(() => { messageElement.style.display = 'none'; }, 500);
                    }, delay);
                }
            }
            autoHideMessage('flashRegisterError', 7000); // Registration errors hide after 7 seconds
        });
    </script>
</body>
</html>

    <script>
        function confirmDelete(classId, className) {
            if (confirm('Are you sure you want to delete the class "' + className + '"?\n\nThis action cannot be undone and may affect associated schedules and bookings.')) {
                window.location.href = '${pageContext.request.contextPath}/admin/manageClasses?action=delete&classId=' + classId;
            }

    <script>
        function confirmDeleteSchedule(scheduleId, location, startTime) {
            if (confirm('Are you sure you want to delete the schedule for:\n\n' +
                       'Location: ' + location + '\n' +
                       'Start Time: ' + startTime + '\n\n' +
                       'This action cannot be undone and may affect existing bookings.')) {
                window.location.href = '${pageContext.request.contextPath}/admin/manageSchedules?action=delete&scheduleId=' + scheduleId;
            }
        }
    </script>

    <script>
        // Set minimum date to current date/time for new schedules
        document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
            const startTimeInput = document.getElementById('startTime');
            const endTimeInput = document.getElementById('endTime');
            
            // Set minimum date to now
            const now = new Date();
            const minDateTime = now.toISOString().slice(0, 16);
            startTimeInput.setAttribute('min', minDateTime);
            endTimeInput.setAttribute('min', minDateTime);
            
            // Update end time minimum when start time changes
            startTimeInput.addEventListener('change', function() {
                endTimeInput.setAttribute('min', this.value);
                
                // If end time is before start time, update it
                if (endTimeInput.value && endTimeInput.value <= this.value) {
                    const startTime = new Date(this.value);
                    startTime.setHours(startTime.getHours() + 1); // Add 1 hour as default duration
                    endTimeInput.value = startTime.toISOString().slice(0, 16);
                }
            });
        });
    </script>

package com.classbooking.dao;

import java.sql.Connection;
import java.sql.PreparedStatement;
import java.sql.ResultSet;
import java.sql.SQLException;
import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.List;

import com.classbooking.model.Booking;

public class BookingDAO {
    public boolean placeBooking(Booking booking) {
        String sql = "INSERT INTO bookings (user_id, class_id, booking_time) VALUES (?, ?, ?)";
        try (Connection conn = DBUtil.getConnection();
             PreparedStatement stmt = conn.prepareStatement(sql)) {
            stmt.setInt(1, booking.getUserId());
            stmt.setInt(2, booking.getClassId());
            stmt.setTimestamp(3, booking.getBookingTime());
            return stmt.executeUpdate() > 0;
        } catch (SQLException e) {
            System.err.println("Error placing booking: " + e.getMessage());
            return false;
        }
    }

    public List<Booking> getBookingsByUser(int userId) {
        List<Booking> bookings = new ArrayList<>();
        String sql = "SELECT * FROM bookings WHERE user_id = ?";
        try (Connection conn = DBUtil.getConnection();
             PreparedStatement stmt = conn.prepareStatement(sql)) {
            stmt.setInt(1, userId);
            ResultSet rs = stmt.executeQuery();
            while (rs.next()) {
                Booking booking = new Booking();
                booking.setId(rs.getInt("id"));
                booking.setUserId(rs.getInt("user_id"));
                booking.setClassId(rs.getInt("class_id"));
                booking.setBookingTime(rs.getTimestamp("booking_time"));
                bookings.add(booking);
            }
        } catch (SQLException e) {
            System.err.println("Error retrieving bookings for user " + userId + ": " + e.getMessage());
        }
        return bookings;
    }
}

File: C:\Users\GUIDE\eclipse-workspace\ClassBookingSystem\src\main\java\com\classbooking\dao\ClassDAO.java

package com.classbooking.dao;

import java.sql.*;
import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.List;
import com.classbooking.model.Class;

public class ClassDAO {

    // SQL queries based on assumed table structure: classes(id, class_name, description, image_url, class_time, capacity)
    private static final String SELECT_ALL_CLASSES = "SELECT id, class_name, description, image_url, class_time, capacity FROM classes";
    private static final String SELECT_CLASS_BY_ID = "SELECT id, class_name, description, image_url, class_time, capacity FROM classes WHERE id = ?";
    private static final String INSERT_CLASS = "INSERT INTO classes (class_name, description, image_url, class_time, capacity) VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?, ?)";
    private static final String UPDATE_CLASS = "UPDATE classes SET class_name = ?, description = ?, image_url = ?, class_time = ?, capacity = ? WHERE id = ?";
    private static final String DELETE_CLASS = "DELETE FROM classes WHERE id = ?";
    public List<Class> getAllClasses() {
        List<Class> classes = new ArrayList<>();
        try (Connection conn = DBUtil.getConnection();
             PreparedStatement pstmt = conn.prepareStatement(SELECT_ALL_CLASSES);
             ResultSet rs = pstmt.executeQuery()) {

            while (rs.next()) {
                Class cls = mapRowToClass(rs);
                classes.add(cls);
            }
        } catch (SQLException e) {
            e.printStackTrace(); // Consider a more robust error handling strategy
        }
        return classes;
    }

    public Class getClassById(int classId) {
        Class cls = null;
        try (Connection conn = DBUtil.getConnection();
             PreparedStatement pstmt = conn.prepareStatement(SELECT_CLASS_BY_ID)) {
            pstmt.setInt(1, classId);
            try (ResultSet rs = pstmt.executeQuery()) {
                if (rs.next()) {
                    cls = mapRowToClass(rs);
                }
            }
        } catch (SQLException e) {
            e.printStackTrace();
        }
        return cls;
    }

    public void addClass(Class cls) {
        try (Connection conn = DBUtil.getConnection();
             PreparedStatement pstmt = conn.prepareStatement(INSERT_CLASS)) {
            pstmt.setString(1, cls.getName());
            pstmt.setString(2, cls.getDescription());
            pstmt.setString(3, cls.getImageUrl());
            pstmt.setTimestamp(4, cls.getDateTime());
            pstmt.setInt(5, cls.getCapacity());
            pstmt.executeUpdate();
        } catch (SQLException e) {
            e.printStackTrace();
        }
    }

    public void updateClass(Class cls) {
        try (Connection conn = DBUtil.getConnection();
             PreparedStatement pstmt = conn.prepareStatement(UPDATE_CLASS)) {
            pstmt.setString(1, cls.getName());
            pstmt.setString(2, cls.getDescription());
            pstmt.setString(3, cls.getImageUrl());
            pstmt.setTimestamp(4, cls.getDateTime());
            pstmt.setInt(5, cls.getCapacity());
            pstmt.setInt(6, cls.getClassId());
            pstmt.executeUpdate();
        } catch (SQLException e) {
            e.printStackTrace();
        }
    }

    public void deleteClass(int classId) {
        try (Connection conn = DBUtil.getConnection();
             PreparedStatement pstmt = conn.prepareStatement(DELETE_CLASS)) {
            pstmt.setInt(1, classId);
            pstmt.executeUpdate();
        } catch (SQLException e) {
            e.printStackTrace();
        }
    }

    private Class mapRowToClass(ResultSet rs) throws SQLException {
        Class cls = new Class();
        cls.setClassId(rs.getInt("id"));
        cls.setName(rs.getString("class_name"));
        cls.setDescription(rs.getString("description"));
        cls.setImageUrl(rs.getString("image_url"));
        cls.setDateTime(rs.getTimestamp("class_time"));
        cls.setCapacity(rs.getInt("capacity"));
        return cls;
    }
}

File: C:\Users\GUIDE\eclipse-workspace\ClassBookingSystem\src\main\java\com\classbooking\dao\DBUtil.java

package com.classbooking.dao;

import com.zaxxer.hikari.HikariConfig;
import com.zaxxer.hikari.HikariDataSource;
import java.sql.Connection;
import java.sql.SQLException;
import java.util.Properties;

public class DBUtil {
    private static HikariDataSource dataSource;

    static {
        try {
            Properties props = new Properties();
            props.load(DBUtil.class.getClassLoader().getResourceAsStream("config.properties"));

            HikariConfig config = new HikariConfig();
            config.setDriverClassName(props.getProperty("db.driver"));
            config.setJdbcUrl(props.getProperty("db.url"));
            config.setUsername(props.getProperty("db.user"));
            config.setPassword(props.getProperty("db.password"));
            config.setMinimumIdle(5);
            config.setMaximumPoolSize(25);
            config.setConnectionTimeout(30000);
            config.setIdleTimeout(600000);
            config.setMaxLifetime(1800000);
            config.addDataSourceProperty("cachePrepStmts", "true");
            config.addDataSourceProperty("prepStmtCacheSize", "250");
            config.addDataSourceProperty("prepStmtCacheSqlLimit", "2048");
            
            dataSource = new HikariDataSource(config);
        } catch (Exception e) {
            throw new ExceptionInInitializerError("Database configuration failed: " + e);
        }
    }

    public static Connection getConnection() throws SQLException {
        return dataSource.getConnection();
    }
}

File: C:\Users\GUIDE\eclipse-workspace\ClassBookingSystem\src\main\java\com\classbooking\dao\UserDAO.java

package com.classbooking.dao;

import java.sql.Connection;
import java.sql.PreparedStatement;
import java.sql.ResultSet;
import java.sql.SQLException;
import java.util.logging.Level;
import java.util.logging.Logger;

import com.classbooking.model.User;

public class UserDAO {
    private static final Logger LOGGER = Logger.getLogger(UserDAO.class.getName());
    
    public User getUserByUsername(String username) {
        String sql = "SELECT * FROM users WHERE username = ?";
        try (Connection conn = DBUtil.getConnection();
             PreparedStatement stmt = conn.prepareStatement(sql)) {
            
            stmt.setString(1, username);
            ResultSet rs = stmt.executeQuery();
            
            if (rs.next()) {
                return extractUserFromResultSet(rs);
            }
        } catch (SQLException e) {
            LOGGER.log(Level.SEVERE, "Error getting user by username: " + username, e);
        }
        return null;
    }

    public boolean addUser(User user) {
        String sql = "INSERT INTO users (username, password, email, full_name, is_admin) VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?, ?)";
        try (Connection conn = DBUtil.getConnection();
             PreparedStatement stmt = conn.prepareStatement(sql)) {
            
            stmt.setString(1, user.getUsername());
            stmt.setString(2, user.getPassword());
            stmt.setString(3, user.getEmail());
            stmt.setString(4, user.getFullName());
            stmt.setBoolean(5, user.isAdmin());
            
            return stmt.executeUpdate() > 0;
        } catch (SQLException e) {
            LOGGER.log(Level.SEVERE, "Error adding user: " + user.getUsername(), e);
            return false;
        }
    }

    public User getUserById(int userId) {
        String sql = "SELECT * FROM users WHERE user_id = ?";
        try (Connection conn = DBUtil.getConnection();
             PreparedStatement stmt = conn.prepareStatement(sql)) {
            
            stmt.setInt(1, userId);
            ResultSet rs = stmt.executeQuery();
            
            if (rs.next()) {
                return extractUserFromResultSet(rs);
            }
        } catch (SQLException e) {
            LOGGER.log(Level.SEVERE, "Error getting user by ID: " + userId, e);
        }
        return null;
    }

    public boolean updateUserProfile(User user) {
        String sql = "UPDATE users SET email = ?, full_name = ? WHERE user_id = ?";
        try (Connection conn = DBUtil.getConnection();
             PreparedStatement stmt = conn.prepareStatement(sql)) {
            
            stmt.setString(1, user.getEmail());
            stmt.setString(2, user.getFullName());
            stmt.setInt(3, user.getUserId());
            
            return stmt.executeUpdate() > 0;
        } catch (SQLException e) {
            LOGGER.log(Level.SEVERE, "Error updating user profile: " + user.getUsername(), e);
            return false;
        }
    }

    private User extractUserFromResultSet(ResultSet rs) throws SQLException {
        User user = new User();
        user.setUserId(rs.getInt("user_id"));
        user.setUsername(rs.getString("username"));
        user.setPassword(rs.getString("password"));
        user.setEmail(rs.getString("email"));
        user.setFullName(rs.getString("full_name"));
        user.setAdmin(rs.getBoolean("is_admin"));
        user.setCreatedAt(rs.getTimestamp("created_at"));
        return user;
    }
}

File: C:\Users\GUIDE\eclipse-workspace\ClassBookingSystem\src\main\java\com\classbooking\filter\AuthenticationFilter.java

package com.classbooking.filter;

import javax.servlet.*;
import javax.servlet.http.HttpServletRequest;
import javax.servlet.http.HttpServletResponse;
import javax.servlet.http.HttpSession;
import java.io.IOException;

public class AuthenticationFilter implements Filter {
    public void init(FilterConfig config) throws ServletException {}

    public void doFilter(ServletRequest request, ServletResponse response, FilterChain chain)
            throws IOException, ServletException {
        HttpServletRequest req = (HttpServletRequest) request;
        HttpServletResponse res = (HttpServletResponse) response;

        HttpSession session = req.getSession(false);
        boolean isLoggedIn = (session != null && session.getAttribute("user") != null);
        boolean isAdmin = (session != null && "admin".equals(session.getAttribute("role")));

        if (isLoggedIn && isAdmin) {
            chain.doFilter(request, response);
        } else {
            res.sendRedirect(req.getContextPath() + "/login.jsp");
        }
    }

    public void destroy() {}
}

File: C:\Users\GUIDE\eclipse-workspace\ClassBookingSystem\src\main\java\com\classbooking\filter\AutoLoginFilter.java

package com.classbooking.filter;

import java.io.IOException;
import java.sql.Connection;
import java.sql.PreparedStatement;
import java.sql.ResultSet;
import java.sql.SQLException;

import javax.servlet.Filter;
import javax.servlet.FilterChain;
import javax.servlet.FilterConfig;
import javax.servlet.ServletException;
import javax.servlet.ServletRequest;
import javax.servlet.ServletResponse;
import javax.servlet.http.Cookie;
import javax.servlet.http.HttpServletRequest;
import javax.servlet.http.HttpSession;

public class AutoLoginFilter implements Filter {
    @Override
    public void init(FilterConfig config) throws ServletException {}

    @Override
    public void doFilter(ServletRequest request, ServletResponse response, FilterChain chain) 
        throws IOException, ServletException {
        HttpServletRequest req = (HttpServletRequest) request;
        Cookie[] cookies = req.getCookies();
        if (cookies != null) {
            for (Cookie cookie : cookies) {
                if (cookie.getName().equals("rememberMe")) {
                    String token = cookie.getValue();
                    try (Connection conn = com.classbooking.dao.DBUtil.getConnection();
                         PreparedStatement stmt = conn.prepareStatement("SELECT * FROM users WHERE remember_token = ?")) {
                        stmt.setString(1, token);
                        ResultSet rs = stmt.executeQuery();
                        if (rs.next()) {
                            HttpSession session = req.getSession(true);
                            session.setAttribute("user", rs.getString("email"));
                            session.setAttribute("role", rs.getString("role"));
                        }
                    } catch (SQLException e) {
                        // Log the error instead of printStackTrace
                        System.err.println("Error validating remember-me token: " + e.getMessage());
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        chain.doFilter(request, response);
    }

    @Override
    public void destroy() {}
}

File: C:\Users\GUIDE\eclipse-workspace\ClassBookingSystem\src\main\java\com\classbooking\service\UserService.java

package com.classbooking.service;

import com.classbooking.dao.UserDAO;
import com.classbooking.model.User;
// For password hashing, you would typically import a library like BCrypt
// import org.mindrot.jbcrypt.BCrypt; // Example if using jBCrypt

public class UserService {
    private final UserDAO userDAO;

    /**
     * Initializes UserDAO instance
     */
    public UserService() {
        this.userDAO = new UserDAO();
    }

    /**
     * Registers a new user.
     * In a real application, this method would handle password hashing.
     * @param username The username.
     * @param password The plain text password.
     * @param email The email address.
     * @param fullName The user's full name.
     * @return true if registration is successful, false otherwise (e.g., username or email already exists).
     */
        /**
     * Registers new user with validation
     * @param username Unique identifier
     * @param password Plain text password
     * @param email User email address
     * @param fullName User's complete name
     * @return Registration success status
     */
    public boolean registerUser(String username, String password, String email, String fullName) {
        if (userDAO.getUserByUsername(username) != null) {
            System.err.println("Registration failed: Username '" + username + "' already exists.");
            return false; 
        }
        // Add email existence check if needed, e.g., if UserDAO has getUserByEmail()

        String storedPassword = password; // In a real app: BCrypt.hashpw(password, BCrypt.gensalt());

        User newUser = new User();
        newUser.setUsername(username);
        newUser.setPassword(storedPassword); 
        newUser.setEmail(email);
        newUser.setFullName(fullName);
        newUser.setAdmin(false); 

        return userDAO.addUser(newUser);
    }

    /**
     * Authenticates a user.
     * Compares plain text password with stored (ideally hashed) password.
     * @param username The username.
     * @param plainTextPassword The plain text password entered by the user.
     * @return The User object if authentication is successful, null otherwise.
     */
    public User loginUser(String username, String plainTextPassword) {
        User user = userDAO.getUserByUsername(username);

        if (user != null) {
            // In a real app with hashing: if (BCrypt.checkpw(plainTextPassword, user.getPassword())) { return user; }
            if (plainTextPassword.equals(user.getPassword())) { // Plain text comparison for lab
                return user; 
            } else {
                System.err.println("Login failed: Incorrect password for user '" + username + "'.");
                return null; 
            }
        }
        System.err.println("Login failed: User '" + username + "' not found.");
        return null; 
    }

    /**
     * Retrieves a user by their username.
     * This is used by the AutoLoginFilter to validate a user from a cookie.
     * @param username The username to search for.
     * @return The User object if found, null otherwise.
     */
    public User getUserByUsername(String username) {
        return userDAO.getUserByUsername(username);
    }

    /**
     * Retrieves user details by user ID.
     * @param userId The ID of the user.
     * @return User object if found, null otherwise.
     */
    public User getUserById(int userId) {
        return userDAO.getUserById(userId);
    }

    public boolean addUser(User user) {
        return userDAO.addUser(user);
    }

    /**
     * Updates a user's profile (e.g., email, full name).
     * @param user The User object with updated information.
     * @return true if successful, false otherwise.
     */
    public boolean updateUserProfile(User user) {
        return userDAO.updateUserProfile(user);
    }
}

package com.classbooking.service.impl;

import com.classbooking.dao.ClassDAO;
import com.classbooking.model.Booking;
import com.classbooking.model.Class;
import com.classbooking.service.BookingService;

import java.sql.Timestamp;
import java.util.List;

public class BookingServiceImpl extends BookingService {
    private ClassDAO classDAO;

    public BookingServiceImpl() {
        super();
        this.classDAO = new ClassDAO();
    }

    /**
     * Places a new booking for a user
     * @param userId The ID of the user making the booking
     * @param classId The ID of the class being booked
     * @return true if booking was successful, false otherwise
     */
    public boolean placeBooking(int userId, int classId) {
        // Check if the class exists and has available capacity
        Class fitnessClass = classDAO.getClassById(classId);
        if (fitnessClass == null || fitnessClass.getCapacity() <= 0) {
            return false;
        }
        
        // Create a new booking
        Booking booking = new Booking();
        booking.setUserId(userId);
        booking.setClassId(classId);
        booking.setBookingTime(new Timestamp(System.currentTimeMillis()));
        
        // Save the booking using the parent class method
        return super.placeBooking(booking);
    }

    /**
     * Gets all bookings for a specific user
     * @param userId The ID of the user
     * @return List of bookings for the user
     */
    public List<Booking> getBookingHistory(int userId) {
        return super.getBookingHistory(userId);
    }
}

package com.classbooking.service.impl;

import com.classbooking.model.User;

     */
    @Override
    public boolean updateUserProfile(User user) {
        return super.updateUserProfile(user);
    }
}

File: C:\Users\GUIDE\eclipse-workspace\ClassBookingSystem\src\main\java\com\classbooking\servlet\BookingServlet.java

package com.classbooking.servlet;

import java.io.IOException;

import javax.servlet.ServletException;
import javax.servlet.annotation.WebServlet;
import javax.servlet.http.HttpServlet;
import javax.servlet.http.HttpServletRequest;
import javax.servlet.http.HttpServletResponse;
import javax.servlet.http.HttpSession;

import com.classbooking.model.Booking;
import com.classbooking.model.Class;
import com.classbooking.model.User;
import com.classbooking.service.BookingService;
import com.classbooking.service.ClassService;
import com.classbooking.service.impl.BookingServiceImpl;
import com.classbooking.service.impl.ClassServiceImpl;

@WebServlet("/booking")
public class BookingServlet extends HttpServlet {
    private static final long serialVersionUID = 1L;
    private ClassService classService;
    private BookingService bookingService;
    
    @Override
    public void init() throws ServletException {
        super.init();
        classService = new ClassServiceImpl();
        bookingService = new BookingServiceImpl();
    }
    
    @Override
    protected void doGet(HttpServletRequest request, HttpServletResponse response) 
            throws ServletException, IOException {
        
        // Get the class ID from the request parameter
        String classIdStr = request.getParameter("classId");
        
        if (classIdStr == null || classIdStr.isEmpty()) {
            request.setAttribute("errorMessage", "No class selected for booking.");
            response.sendRedirect(request.getContextPath() + "/classes");
            return;
        }
        
        try {
            int classId = Integer.parseInt(classIdStr);
            
            // Get the class details
            Class selectedClass = classService.getClassById(classId);
            
            if (selectedClass == null) {
                request.setAttribute("errorMessage", "Selected class not found.");
                response.sendRedirect(request.getContextPath() + "/classes");
                return;
            }
            
            // Check if user is logged in
            HttpSession session = request.getSession(false);
            if (session == null || session.getAttribute("loggedInUser") == null) {
                // Store the class ID in session for redirect after login
                session = request.getSession(true);
                session.setAttribute("pendingBookingClassId", classId);
                response.sendRedirect(request.getContextPath() + "/login.jsp");
                return;
            }
            
            // Set the class in request attribute and forward to confirmation page
            request.setAttribute("selectedClass", selectedClass);
            request.getRequestDispatcher("/confirmBooking.jsp").forward(request, response);
            
        } catch (NumberFormatException e) {
            request.setAttribute("errorMessage", "Invalid class ID format.");
            response.sendRedirect(request.getContextPath() + "/classes");
        }
    }
    
    @Override
    protected void doPost(HttpServletRequest request, HttpServletResponse response) 
            throws ServletException, IOException {
        // Get the class ID from the request parameter
        String classIdStr = request.getParameter("classId");
        
        if (classIdStr == null || classIdStr.isEmpty()) {
            request.setAttribute("errorMessage", "No class selected for booking.");
            response.sendRedirect(request.getContextPath() + "/classes");
            return;
        }
        
        try {
            int classId = Integer.parseInt(classIdStr);
            
            // Get the user from the session
            HttpSession session = request.getSession(false);
            if (session == null || session.getAttribute("loggedInUser") == null) {
                response.sendRedirect(request.getContextPath() + "/login.jsp");
                return;
            }
            
            User user = (User) session.getAttribute("loggedInUser");
            
            // Create a Booking object
            Booking booking = new Booking();
            booking.setUserId(user.getUserId());
            booking.setClassId(classId);
            
            // Place the booking using the booking service
            boolean success = bookingService.placeBooking(booking);
            
            if (success) {
                // Redirect to booking success page
                request.setAttribute("bookingSuccess", true);
                request.setAttribute("classId", classId);
                request.getRequestDispatcher("/confirmBooking.jsp").forward(request, response);
            } else {
                // Redirect to error page
                request.setAttribute("errorMessage", "Failed to book the class. Please try again.");
                response.sendRedirect(request.getContextPath() + "/classes");
            }
            
        } catch (NumberFormatException e) {
            request.setAttribute("errorMessage", "Invalid class ID format.");
            response.sendRedirect(request.getContextPath() + "/classes");
        }
    }
}

File: C:\Users\GUIDE\eclipse-workspace\ClassBookingSystem\src\main\java\com\classbooking\servlet\LoginServlet.java

package com.classbooking.servlet;

import java.io.IOException;

import javax.servlet.ServletException;
import javax.servlet.annotation.WebServlet;
import javax.servlet.http.HttpServlet;
import javax.servlet.http.HttpServletRequest;
import javax.servlet.http.HttpServletResponse;
import javax.servlet.http.HttpSession;

import com.classbooking.model.User;
import com.classbooking.service.UserService;
import com.classbooking.service.impl.UserServiceImpl;

@WebServlet("/login")
public class LoginServlet extends HttpServlet {
    private static final long serialVersionUID = 1L;
    private UserService userService;
    
    @Override
    public void init() throws ServletException {
        super.init();
        userService = new UserServiceImpl();
    }
    
    @Override
    protected void doGet(HttpServletRequest request, HttpServletResponse response) 
            throws ServletException, IOException {
        // Check if user is already logged in
        HttpSession session = request.getSession(false);
        if (session != null && session.getAttribute("loggedInUser") != null) {
            // User is already logged in, redirect to classes page
            response.sendRedirect(request.getContextPath() + "/classes");
            return;
        }
        
        // Forward to login page
        request.getRequestDispatcher("/login.jsp").forward(request, response);
    }
    
    @Override
    protected void doPost(HttpServletRequest request, HttpServletResponse response) 
            throws ServletException, IOException {
        String username = request.getParameter("username");
        String password = request.getParameter("password");
        String rememberMe = request.getParameter("rememberMe");
        
        // Validate input
        if (username == null || username.trim().isEmpty() || password == null || password.trim().isEmpty()) {
            request.setAttribute("errorMessage", "Username and password are required");
            request.getRequestDispatcher("/login.jsp").forward(request, response);
            return;
        }
        
        try {
            // Authenticate user
            User user = userService.loginUser(username, password);
            
            if (user != null) {
                // Create session and store user
                HttpSession session = request.getSession(true);
                session.setAttribute("loggedInUser", user);
                
                // Set remember-me cookie if requested
                if ("on".equals(rememberMe)) {
                    // Implementation for remember-me functionality would go here
                    // This typically involves creating a secure token and storing it in a cookie
                }
                
                // Check if there was a pending booking
                Integer pendingBookingClassId = (Integer) session.getAttribute("pendingBookingClassId");
                if (pendingBookingClassId != null) {
                    session.removeAttribute("pendingBookingClassId");
                    response.sendRedirect(request.getContextPath() + "/booking?classId=" + pendingBookingClassId);
                    return;
                }
                
                // Redirect to classes page
                response.sendRedirect(request.getContextPath() + "/classes");
            } else {
                // Authentication failed
                request.setAttribute("errorMessage", "Invalid username or password");
                request.getRequestDispatcher("/login.jsp").forward(request, response);
            }
        } catch (IOException | ServletException e) {
            // Handle these specific exceptions
            request.setAttribute("errorMessage", "System error: " + e.getMessage());
            request.getRequestDispatcher("/login.jsp").forward(request, response);
        } catch (RuntimeException e) {
            // Handle runtime exceptions (e.g., database connection issues)
            request.setAttribute("errorMessage", "System error: Please try again later.");
            request.getRequestDispatcher("/login.jsp").forward(request, response);
        }
    }
}

File: C:\Users\GUIDE\eclipse-workspace\ClassBookingSystem\src\main\java\com\classbooking\servlet\ManageClassesServlet.java

package com.classbooking.servlet;

import com.classbooking.model.Class;
import com.classbooking.service.ClassService;
import com.classbooking.service.impl.ClassServiceImpl;

import javax.servlet.ServletException;
import javax.servlet.annotation.WebServlet;
import javax.servlet.http.HttpServlet;
import javax.servlet.http.HttpServletRequest;
import javax.servlet.http.HttpServletResponse;
import java.io.IOException;
import java.util.List;
import java.sql.Timestamp;
import java.text.SimpleDateFormat;
import java.text.ParseException;

@WebServlet("/admin/manageClasses")
public class ManageClassesServlet extends HttpServlet {
    private static final long serialVersionUID = 1L;
    
    private ClassService classService;

    @Override
    public void init() throws ServletException {
        super.init();
        // Initialize the ClassService (assuming dependency injection or manual instantiation)
        classService = new ClassServiceImpl(); // Replace with proper dependency injection if used
    }

    @Override
    protected void doGet(HttpServletRequest request, HttpServletResponse response) throws ServletException, IOException {
        String action = request.getParameter("action");

        if (action == null) {
            action = "list"; // Default action
        }

        try {
            switch (action) {
                case "list":
                    listClasses(request, response);
                    break;
                case "showAddForm":
                    showAddForm(request, response);
                    break;
                case "showEditForm":
                    showEditForm(request, response);
                    break;
                case "deleteClass":
                    deleteClass(request, response);
                    break;
                default:
                    listClasses(request, response);
                    break;
            }
        } catch (Exception ex) {
            throw new ServletException(ex);
        }
    }

    @Override
    protected void doPost(HttpServletRequest request, HttpServletResponse response) throws ServletException, IOException {
        String formAction = request.getParameter("formAction");

        try {
            switch (formAction) {
                case "addClass":
                    addClass(request, response);
                    break;
                case "updateClass":
                    updateClass(request, response);
                    break;
                default:
                    // Handle unknown form action or redirect to list
                    response.sendRedirect(request.getContextPath() + "/admin/manageClasses");
                    break;
            }
        } catch (Exception ex) {
            throw new ServletException(ex);
        }
    }

    private void listClasses(HttpServletRequest request, HttpServletResponse response) throws ServletException, IOException {
        List<Class> classes = classService.getAllClasses();
        request.setAttribute("classes", classes);
        request.getRequestDispatcher("/admin/listClasses.jsp").forward(request, response);
    }

    private void showAddForm(HttpServletRequest request, HttpServletResponse response) throws ServletException, IOException {
        request.getRequestDispatcher("/admin/classForm.jsp").forward(request, response);
    }

    private void showEditForm(HttpServletRequest request, HttpServletResponse response) throws ServletException, IOException {
        int classId = Integer.parseInt(request.getParameter("classId"));
        Class classToEdit = classService.getClassById(classId);
        request.setAttribute("classToEdit", classToEdit);
        request.getRequestDispatcher("/admin/classForm.jsp").forward(request, response);
    }

    private void addClass(HttpServletRequest request, HttpServletResponse response) throws ServletException, IOException {
        String name = request.getParameter("name");
        String description = request.getParameter("description");
        String imageUrl = request.getParameter("imageUrl");
        String dateTimeStr = request.getParameter("dateTime");
        String capacityStr = request.getParameter("capacity");

        Class newClass = new Class();
        newClass.setName(name);
        newClass.setDescription(description);
        newClass.setImageUrl(imageUrl);

        try {
            if (dateTimeStr != null && !dateTimeStr.isEmpty()) {
                SimpleDateFormat dateFormat = new SimpleDateFormat("yyyy-MM-dd HH:mm:ss");
                java.util.Date parsedDate = dateFormat.parse(dateTimeStr);
                newClass.setDateTime(new Timestamp(parsedDate.getTime()));
            } else {
                // Handle missing dateTime: set to null or a default, or raise error
                // For now, assuming DAO/DB handles null if column is nullable, or this is an error condition
                 newClass.setDateTime(null); // Or throw an error if it's mandatory
            }
            if (capacityStr != null && !capacityStr.isEmpty()) {
                newClass.setCapacity(Integer.parseInt(capacityStr));
            } else {
                // Handle missing capacity: set to 0 or a default, or raise error
                newClass.setCapacity(0); // Or throw an error if 0 is invalid / it's mandatory
            }

            classService.addClass(newClass);
            request.setAttribute("successMessage", "Class added successfully!");
        } catch (ParseException e) {
            request.setAttribute("errorMessage", "Error adding class: Invalid date format (expected yyyy-MM-dd HH:mm:ss). " + e.getMessage());
            // Log e for debugging
        } catch (NumberFormatException e) {
            request.setAttribute("errorMessage", "Error adding class: Invalid capacity format. " + e.getMessage());
            // Log e for debugging
        } catch (Exception e) {
            request.setAttribute("errorMessage", "Error adding class: " + e.getMessage());
            // Log e for debugging
        }

        listClasses(request, response); // Redirect back to the list
    }

    private void updateClass(HttpServletRequest request, HttpServletResponse response) throws ServletException, IOException {
        int classId = Integer.parseInt(request.getParameter("classId"));
        Class classToUpdate = classService.getClassById(classId);

        if (classToUpdate == null) {
            request.setAttribute("errorMessage", "Error updating class: Class with ID " + classId + " not found.");
            listClasses(request, response);
            return;
        }

        String name = request.getParameter("name");
        String description = request.getParameter("description");
        String imageUrl = request.getParameter("imageUrl");
        String dateTimeStr = request.getParameter("dateTime");
        String capacityStr = request.getParameter("capacity");

        // Update fields from request parameters. If a parameter is not provided or empty,
        // the existing value in classToUpdate (fetched from DB) will be retained.
        if (name != null && !name.isEmpty()) {
            classToUpdate.setName(name);
        }
        if (description != null && !description.isEmpty()) {
            classToUpdate.setDescription(description);
        }
        if (imageUrl != null) { // Allow setting empty string for imageUrl to clear it
            classToUpdate.setImageUrl(imageUrl);
        }

        try {
            if (dateTimeStr != null && !dateTimeStr.isEmpty()) {
                SimpleDateFormat dateFormat = new SimpleDateFormat("yyyy-MM-dd HH:mm:ss");
                java.util.Date parsedDate = dateFormat.parse(dateTimeStr);
                classToUpdate.setDateTime(new Timestamp(parsedDate.getTime()));
            } else if (dateTimeStr != null && dateTimeStr.isEmpty()) {
                 // If form submitted an empty string for dateTime, explicitly set to null if desired
                 // classToUpdate.setDateTime(null); 
                 // Otherwise, if not touched, existing value remains. Current DAO updates all fields.
                 // For safety, if it's meant to be cleared, it should be explicitly set to null.
                 // For now, if empty, it means "don't change". But DAO will use current value.
            }

            if (capacityStr != null && !capacityStr.isEmpty()) {
                classToUpdate.setCapacity(Integer.parseInt(capacityStr));
            }

            classService.updateClass(classToUpdate);
            request.setAttribute("successMessage", "Class updated successfully!");
        } catch (ParseException e) {
            request.setAttribute("errorMessage", "Error updating class: Invalid date format (expected yyyy-MM-dd HH:mm:ss). " + e.getMessage());
            // Log e for debugging
        } catch (NumberFormatException e) {
            request.setAttribute("errorMessage", "Error updating class: Invalid capacity format. " + e.getMessage());
            // Log e for debugging
        } catch (Exception e) {
            request.setAttribute("errorMessage", "Error updating class: " + e.getMessage());
            // Log e for debugging
        }

        listClasses(request, response); // Redirect back to the list
    }

    private void deleteClass(HttpServletRequest request, HttpServletResponse response) throws ServletException, IOException {
        int classId = Integer.parseInt(request.getParameter("classId"));

        try {
            classService.deleteClass(classId);
            request.setAttribute("successMessage", "Class deleted successfully!");
        } catch (Exception e) {
            request.setAttribute("errorMessage", "Error deleting class: " + e.getMessage());
        }

        listClasses(request, response); // Redirect back to the list
    }
}

package com.classbooking.servlet;

import java.io.IOException;
import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.List;

import javax.servlet.ServletException;
import javax.servlet.annotation.WebServlet;
import javax.servlet.http.HttpServlet;
import javax.servlet.http.HttpServletRequest;
import javax.servlet.http.HttpServletResponse;
import javax.servlet.http.HttpSession;

import com.classbooking.model.Booking;
import com.classbooking.model.Class;
import com.classbooking.model.User;
import com.classbooking.service.BookingService;
import com.classbooking.service.ClassService;
import com.classbooking.service.impl.BookingServiceImpl;
import com.classbooking.service.impl.ClassServiceImpl;

@WebServlet("/myBookings")
public class MyBookingsServlet extends HttpServlet {
    private static final long serialVersionUID = 1L;
    private BookingService bookingService;
    private ClassService classService;
    
    @Override
    public void init() throws ServletException {
        super.init();
        bookingService = new BookingServiceImpl();
        classService = new ClassServiceImpl();
    }
    
    @Override
    protected void doGet(HttpServletRequest request, HttpServletResponse response) 
            throws ServletException, IOException {
        
        // Check if user is logged in
        HttpSession session = request.getSession(false);
        if (session == null || session.getAttribute("loggedInUser") == null) {
            response.sendRedirect(request.getContextPath() + "/login.jsp");
            return;
        }
        
        User user = (User) session.getAttribute("loggedInUser");
        
        // Get user's bookings
        List<Booking> bookings = bookingService.getBookingHistory(user.getUserId());
        
        // Create a list to store booking details with class information
        List<BookingDetail> bookingDetails = new ArrayList<>();
        
        // For each booking, get the class details
        for (Booking booking : bookings) {
            Class fitnessClass = classService.getClassById(booking.getClassId());
            if (fitnessClass != null) {
                BookingDetail detail = new BookingDetail();
                detail.setBooking(booking);
                detail.setFitnessClass(fitnessClass);
                bookingDetails.add(detail);
            }
        }
        
        // Set the booking details in request attribute
        request.setAttribute("bookingDetails", bookingDetails);
        
        // Forward to the my bookings page
        request.getRequestDispatcher("/myBookings.jsp").forward(request, response);
    }
    
    // Inner class to hold booking details with class information
    public static class BookingDetail {
        private Booking booking;
        private Class fitnessClass;
        
        public Booking getBooking() { return booking; }
        public void setBooking(Booking booking) { this.booking = booking; }
        
        public Class getFitnessClass() { return fitnessClass; }
        public void setFitnessClass(Class fitnessClass) { this.fitnessClass = fitnessClass; }
    }
}

File: C:\Users\GUIDE\eclipse-workspace\ClassBookingSystem\src\main\resources\db_scripts.sql

-- Database schema for Class Booking System
CREATE DATABASE IF NOT EXISTS classdb;
USE classdb;

-- Users table
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS users (
    id INT AUTO_INCREMENT PRIMARY KEY,
    username VARCHAR(50) UNIQUE NOT NULL,
    password VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
    is_admin BOOLEAN DEFAULT FALSE
) ENGINE=InnoDB;

-- Classes table
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS classes (
    id INT AUTO_INCREMENT PRIMARY KEY,
    class_name VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    class_time DATETIME NOT NULL,
    capacity INT NOT NULL
) ENGINE=InnoDB;

-- Bookings table
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS bookings (
    id INT AUTO_INCREMENT PRIMARY KEY,
    user_id INT NOT NULL,
    class_id INT NOT NULL,
    booking_time TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    FOREIGN KEY (user_id) REFERENCES users(id),
    FOREIGN KEY (class_id) REFERENCES classes(id)
) ENGINE=InnoDB;

-- Sample data
INSERT INTO users (username, password, is_admin) VALUES
('admin', 'admin123', TRUE),
('user1', 'pass123', FALSE);

INSERT INTO classes (class_name, class_time, capacity) VALUES
('Yoga Basics', '2024-06-01 10:00:00', 20),
('Advanced Pilates', '2024-06-02 14:00:00', 15);

-- Indexes for better performance
CREATE INDEX idx_class_time ON classes(class_time);
CREATE INDEX idx_booking_user ON bookings(user_id);

    <script type="text/javascript">
        document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
            function autoHideMessage(elementId, delay) {
                const messageElement = document.getElementById(elementId);
                if (messageElement && messageElement.classList.contains('show')) {
                    setTimeout(function() {
                        var alertInstance = bootstrap.Alert.getInstance(messageElement);
                        if (alertInstance) {
                            alertInstance.close();
                        } else {
                            messageElement.style.display = 'none';
                        }
                    }, delay);
                }
            }
            autoHideMessage('flashSuccessMessage', 5000); // Success messages hide after 5 seconds
            autoHideMessage('flashErrorMessage', 7000);  // Error messages hide after 7 seconds
        });
    </script>
</body>
</html>

    <script>
        // Form validation
        (function () {
            'use strict'
            var forms = document.querySelectorAll('.needs-validation')
            Array.prototype.slice.call(forms)
                .forEach(function (form) {
                    form.addEventListener('submit', function (event) {
                        if (!form.checkValidity()) {
                            event.preventDefault()
                            event.stopPropagation()
                        }
                        form.classList.add('was-validated')
                    }, false)
                })
        })()
    </script>

    <script type="text/javascript">
        document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
            function autoHideMessage(elementId, delay) {
                const messageElement = document.getElementById(elementId);
                if (messageElement && messageElement.classList.contains('show')) {
                    setTimeout(function() {
                        var alertInstance = bootstrap.Alert.getInstance(messageElement);
                        if (alertInstance) {
                            alertInstance.close();
                        } else {
                            messageElement.style.transition = 'opacity 0.5s ease-out';
                            messageElement.style.opacity = '0';
                            setTimeout(() => { messageElement.style.display = 'none'; }, 500);
                        }
                    }, delay);
                } else if (messageElement) { 
                     setTimeout(function() {
                        messageElement.style.transition = 'opacity 0.5s ease-out';
                        messageElement.style.opacity = '0';
                        setTimeout(() => { messageElement.style.display = 'none'; }, 500);
                    }, delay);
                }
            }
            autoHideMessage('flashMyBookingsPageError', 7000); // For page-specific errors
            autoHideMessage('flashMyBookingsSuccess', 5000); // For success messages from session
        });
    </script>
</body>
</html>

                        </div>
                        <div class="col-md-3">
                            <h3 class="mb-1"><c:out value="${cancelledCount}"/></h3>
                            <small>Cancelled</small>
                        </div>
                        <div class="col-md-3">
                            <h3 class="mb-1"><c:out value="${pendingCount}"/></h3>
                            <small>Pending</small>
                        </div>
                    </div>
                </div>
            </div>
        </c:if>

        <div class="card">
            <div class="card-header">
                <h5 class="mb-0"><i class="fas fa-list me-2"></i>Booking Details</h5>
            </div>
            <div class="card-body">
                <c:choose>
                    <c:when test="${not empty allBookings}">
                        <div class="table-responsive">
                            <table class="table table-striped table-hover">
                                <thead class="table-dark">
                                    <tr>
                                        <th scope="col">Booking ID</th>
                                        <th scope="col">User</th>
                                        <th scope="col">Class Title</th>
                                        <th scope="col">Schedule</th>
                                        <th scope="col">Location</th>
                                        <th scope="col">Booking Time</th>
                                        <th scope="col">Status</th>
                                    </tr>
                                </thead>
                                <tbody>
                                    <c:forEach var="booking" items="${allBookings}">
                                        <tr>
                                            <td><c:out value="${booking.bookingId}"/></td>
                                            <td>
                                                <strong><c:out value="${booking.user.username}"/></strong>
                                                <br><small class="text-muted"><c:out value="${booking.user.email}"/></small>
                                            </td>
                                            <td>
                                                <strong><c:out value="${booking.classSchedule.classInfo.title}"/></strong>
                                                <br><small class="text-muted">Instructor: <c:out value="${booking.classSchedule.classInfo.instructor}"/></small>
                                            </td>
                                            <td><c:out value="${booking.classSchedule.scheduleTime}"/></td>
                                            <td><c:out value="${booking.classSchedule.location}"/></td>
                                            <td><fmt:formatDate value="${booking.bookingTime}" pattern="yyyy-MM-dd HH:mm"/></td>
                                            <td>
                                                <c:choose>
                                                    <c:when test="${booking.status == 'CONFIRMED'}">
                                                        <span class="status-confirmed"><c:out value="${booking.status}"/></span>
                                                    </c:when>
                                                    <c:when test="${booking.status == 'CANCELLED'}">
                                                        <span class="status-cancelled"><c:out value="${booking.status}"/></span>
                                                    </c:when>
                                                    <c:otherwise>
                                                        <span class="status-pending"><c:out value="${booking.status}"/></span>
                                                    </c:otherwise>
                                                </c:choose>
                                            </td>
                                        </tr>
                                    </c:forEach>
                                </tbody>
                            </table>
                        </div>
                    </c:when>
                    <c:otherwise>
                        <p>No bookings found.</p>
                    </c:otherwise>
                </c:choose>
            </div>
        </div>
    </main>

    <script src="https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/npm/bootstrap@5.3.2/dist/js/bootstrap.bundle.min.js"></script>

                                            </c:when>

                                        <a href="${pageContext.request.contextPath}/admin/manageClasses?action=showEditForm&classId=${classInfo.classId}" 
                                           class="btn btn-warning btn-sm" title="Edit Class">
                                            <i class="fas fa-edit"></i>
                                        </a>
                                        <button type="button" class="btn btn-danger btn-sm" title="Delete Class"
                                                onclick="confirmDelete(${classInfo.classId}, '<c:out value="${classInfo.title}" escapeXml="true"/>')">
                                            <i class="fas fa-trash"></i>
                                        </button>
                                    </td>
                                </tr>
                            </c:forEach>

        function confirmDelete(classId, className) {

                window.location.href = '${pageContext.request.contextPath}/admin/manageClasses?action=delete&classId=' + classId;
            }

    <script src="https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/npm/bootstrap@5.3.2/dist/js/bootstrap.bundle.min.js"></script>
    <script>
        // Set minimum date to current date/time for new schedules
        document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
            const startTimeInput = document.getElementById('startTime');
            const endTimeInput = document.getElementById('endTime');
            
            // Set minimum date to now
            const now = new Date();
            const minDateTime = now.toISOString().slice(0, 16);
            startTimeInput.setAttribute('min', minDateTime);
            endTimeInput.setAttribute('min', minDateTime);
            
            // Update end time minimum when start time changes
            startTimeInput.addEventListener('change', function() {
                endTimeInput.setAttribute('min', this.value);
                
                // If end time is before start time, update it
                if (endTimeInput.value && endTimeInput.value <= this.value) {
                    const startTime = new Date(this.value);
                    startTime.setHours(startTime.getHours() + 1); // Add 1 hour as default duration
                    endTimeInput.value = startTime.toISOString().slice(0, 16);
                }
            });
        });
    </script>
</body>

<?xml version="1.0" encoding="UTF-8" ?>

<taglib xmlns="http://java.sun.com/xml/ns/j2ee"
  xmlns:xsi="http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema-instance"
  xsi:schemaLocation="http://java.sun.com/xml/ns/j2ee http://java.sun.com/xml/ns/j2ee/web-jsptaglibrary_2_0.xsd"
  version="2.0">
    
  <description>JSTL 1.1 functions library</description>
  <display-name>JSTL functions</display-name>
  <tlib-version>1.1</tlib-version>
  <short-name>fn</short-name>
  <uri>http://java.sun.com/jsp/jstl/functions</uri>

  <function>
    <description>
      Tests if an input string contains the specified substring.
    </description>
    <name>contains</name>
    <function-class>org.apache.taglibs.standard.functions.Functions</function-class>
    <function-signature>boolean contains(java.lang.String, java.lang.String)</function-signature>
    <example>
      &lt;c:if test="${fn:contains(name, searchString)}">
    </example>
  </function>

  <function>
    <description>
      Tests if an input string contains the specified substring in a case insensitive way.
    </description>
    <name>containsIgnoreCase</name>
    <function-class>org.apache.taglibs.standard.functions.Functions</function-class>
    <function-signature>boolean containsIgnoreCase(java.lang.String, java.lang.String)</function-signature>
    <example>
      &lt;c:if test="${fn:containsIgnoreCase(name, searchString)}">
    </example>
  </function>

  <function>
    <description>
      Tests if an input string ends with the specified suffix.
    </description>
    <name>endsWith</name>
    <function-class>org.apache.taglibs.standard.functions.Functions</function-class>
    <function-signature>boolean endsWith(java.lang.String, java.lang.String)</function-signature>
    <example>
      &lt;c:if test="${fn:endsWith(filename, ".txt")}">
    </example>
  </function>

  <function>
    <description>
      Escapes characters that could be interpreted as XML markup.
    </description>
    <name>escapeXml</name>
    <function-class>org.apache.taglibs.standard.functions.Functions</function-class>
    <function-signature>java.lang.String escapeXml(java.lang.String)</function-signature>
    <example>
      ${fn:escapeXml(param:info)}
    </example>
  </function>

  <function>
    <description>
      Returns the index withing a string of the first occurrence of a specified substring.
    </description>
    <name>indexOf</name>
    <function-class>org.apache.taglibs.standard.functions.Functions</function-class>
    <function-signature>int indexOf(java.lang.String, java.lang.String)</function-signature>
    <example>
      ${fn:indexOf(name, "-")}
    </example>
  </function>

  <function>
    <description>
      Joins all elements of an array into a string.
    </description>
    <name>join</name>
    <function-class>org.apache.taglibs.standard.functions.Functions</function-class>
    <function-signature>java.lang.String join(java.lang.String[], java.lang.String)</function-signature>
    <example>
      ${fn:join(array, ";")}
    </example>
  </function>

  <function>
    <description>
      Returns the number of items in a collection, or the number of characters in a string.
    </description>
    <name>length</name>
    <function-class>org.apache.taglibs.standard.functions.Functions</function-class>
    <function-signature>int length(java.lang.Object)</function-signature>
    <example>
      You have ${fn:length(shoppingCart.products)} in your shopping cart.
    </example>
  </function>

  <function>
    <description>
      Returns a string resulting from replacing in an input string all occurrences
      of a "before" string into an "after" substring.
    </description>
    <name>replace</name>

    <script type="text/javascript">
        document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
            function autoHideMessage(elementId, delay) {
                const messageElement = document.getElementById(elementId);
                if (messageElement && messageElement.classList.contains('show')) {
                    setTimeout(function() {
                        var alertInstance = bootstrap.Alert.getInstance(messageElement);
                        if (alertInstance) {
                            alertInstance.close();
                        } else {
                            messageElement.style.display = 'none';
                        }
                    }, delay);
                }
            }
            autoHideMessage('flashSuccessMessage', 5000); // Success messages hide after 5 seconds
            autoHideMessage('flashErrorMessage', 7000);  // Error messages hide after 7 seconds
        });
    </script>

    <script>
        // Form validation
        (function () {
            'use strict'
            var forms = document.querySelectorAll('.needs-validation')
            Array.prototype.slice.call(forms)
                .forEach(function (form) {
                    form.addEventListener('submit', function (event) {
                        if (!form.checkValidity()) {
                            event.preventDefault()
                            event.stopPropagation()
                        }
                        form.classList.add('was-validated')
                    }, false)
                })
        })()
    </script>

    <script type="text/javascript">
        document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
            function autoHideMessage(elementId, delay) {
                const messageElement = document.getElementById(elementId);
                if (messageElement && messageElement.classList.contains('show')) {
                    setTimeout(function() {
                        var alertInstance = bootstrap.Alert.getInstance(messageElement);
                        if (alertInstance) {
                            alertInstance.close();
                        } else {
                            messageElement.style.transition = 'opacity 0.5s ease-out';
                            messageElement.style.opacity = '0';
                            setTimeout(() => { messageElement.style.display = 'none'; }, 500);
                        }
                    }, delay);
                } else if (messageElement) { 
                     setTimeout(function() {
                        messageElement.style.transition = 'opacity 0.5s ease-out';
                        messageElement.style.opacity = '0';
                        setTimeout(() => { messageElement.style.display = 'none'; }, 500);
                    }, delay);
                }
            }
            autoHideMessage('flashMyBookingsPageError', 7000); // For page-specific errors
            autoHideMessage('flashMyBookingsSuccess', 5000); // For success messages from session
        });
    </script>

                                                <strong><c:out value="${booking.user.username}"/></strong>

                                            </td>

                                            </td>
                                            <td><c:out value="${booking.classSchedule.scheduleTime}"/></td>
                                            <td><c:out value="${booking.classSchedule.location}"/></td>
                                            <td><fmt:formatDate value="${booking.bookingTime}" pattern="yyyy-MM-dd HH:mm"/></td>
                                            <td>
                                                <c:choose>
                                                    <c:when test="${booking.status == 'CONFIRMED'}">
                                                        <span class="status-confirmed"><c:out value="${booking.status}"/></span>
                                                    </c:when>
                                                    <c:when test="${booking.status == 'CANCELLED'}">
                                                        <span class="status-cancelled"><c:out value="${booking.status}"/></span>
                                                    </c:when>
                                                    <c:otherwise>

                                                    </c:otherwise>
                                                </c:choose>
                                            </td>
                                        </tr>

                            </table>
                        </div>
                    </c:when>
                    <c:otherwise>
                        <p>No bookings found.</p>
                    </c:otherwise>
                </c:choose>
            </div>

        function confirmDelete(classId, className) {
            if (confirm('Are you sure you want to delete the class "' + className + '"?\n\nThis action cannot be undone and may affect associated schedules and bookings.')) {

        function confirmDeleteSchedule(scheduleId, location, startTime) {
            if (confirm('Are you sure you want to delete the schedule for:\n\n' +
                       'Location: ' + location + '\n' +
                       'Start Time: ' + startTime + '\n\n' +
                       'This action cannot be undone and may affect existing bookings.')) {

            }
        }

    <script>
        // Set minimum date to current date/time for new schedules
        document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
            const startTimeInput = document.getElementById('startTime');
            const endTimeInput = document.getElementById('endTime');
            
            // Set minimum date to now
            const now = new Date();
            const minDateTime = now.toISOString().slice(0, 16);
            startTimeInput.setAttribute('min', minDateTime);
            endTimeInput.setAttribute('min', minDateTime);
            
            // Update end time minimum when start time changes
            startTimeInput.addEventListener('change', function() {
                endTimeInput.setAttribute('min', this.value);
                
                // If end time is before start time, update it
                if (endTimeInput.value && endTimeInput.value <= this.value) {
                    const startTime = new Date(this.value);
                    startTime.setHours(startTime.getHours() + 1); // Add 1 hour as default duration
                    endTimeInput.value = startTime.toISOString().slice(0, 16);
                }
            });
        });
    </script>
</body>
</html>

File: C:\Users\GUIDE\eclipse-workspace\ClassBookingSystem\target\ClassBookingSystem-1.0-SNAPSHOT\WEB-INF\classes\db_scripts.sql

-- Database schema for Class Booking System
CREATE DATABASE IF NOT EXISTS classdb;
USE classdb;

-- Users table
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS users (
    id INT AUTO_INCREMENT PRIMARY KEY,
    username VARCHAR(50) UNIQUE NOT NULL,
    password VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
    is_admin BOOLEAN DEFAULT FALSE
) ENGINE=InnoDB;

-- Classes table
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS classes (
    id INT AUTO_INCREMENT PRIMARY KEY,
    class_name VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    class_time DATETIME NOT NULL,
    capacity INT NOT NULL
) ENGINE=InnoDB;

-- Bookings table
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS bookings (
    id INT AUTO_INCREMENT PRIMARY KEY,
    user_id INT NOT NULL,
    class_id INT NOT NULL,
    booking_time TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    FOREIGN KEY (user_id) REFERENCES users(id),
    FOREIGN KEY (class_id) REFERENCES classes(id)
) ENGINE=InnoDB;

-- Sample data
INSERT INTO users (username, password, is_admin) VALUES
('admin', 'admin123', TRUE),
('user1', 'pass123', FALSE);

INSERT INTO classes (class_name, class_time, capacity) VALUES
('Yoga Basics', '2024-06-01 10:00:00', 20),
('Advanced Pilates', '2024-06-02 14:00:00', 15);

-- Indexes for better performance
CREATE INDEX idx_class_time ON classes(class_time);
CREATE INDEX idx_booking_user ON bookings(user_id);

  </function>

File: C:\Users\GUIDE\eclipse-workspace\ClassBookingSystem\target\classes\db_scripts.sql

-- Database schema for Class Booking System
CREATE DATABASE IF NOT EXISTS classdb;
USE classdb;

-- Users table
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS users (
    id INT AUTO_INCREMENT PRIMARY KEY,
    username VARCHAR(50) UNIQUE NOT NULL,
    password VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
    is_admin BOOLEAN DEFAULT FALSE
) ENGINE=InnoDB;

-- Classes table
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS classes (
    id INT AUTO_INCREMENT PRIMARY KEY,
    class_name VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    class_time DATETIME NOT NULL,
    capacity INT NOT NULL
) ENGINE=InnoDB;

-- Bookings table
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS bookings (
    id INT AUTO_INCREMENT PRIMARY KEY,
    user_id INT NOT NULL,
    class_id INT NOT NULL,
    booking_time TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    FOREIGN KEY (user_id) REFERENCES users(id),
    FOREIGN KEY (class_id) REFERENCES classes(id)
) ENGINE=InnoDB;

-- Sample data
INSERT INTO users (username, password, is_admin) VALUES
('admin', 'admin123', TRUE),
('user1', 'pass123', FALSE);

INSERT INTO classes (class_name, class_time, capacity) VALUES
('Yoga Basics', '2024-06-01 10:00:00', 20),
('Advanced Pilates', '2024-06-02 14:00:00', 15);

-- Indexes for better performance
CREATE INDEX idx_class_time ON classes(class_time);
CREATE INDEX idx_booking_user ON bookings(user_id);

<taglib xmlns="http://java.sun.com/xml/ns/j2ee"
  xmlns:xsi="http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema-instance"
  xsi:schemaLocation="http://java.sun.com/xml/ns/j2ee http://java.sun.com/xml/ns/j2ee/web-jsptaglibrary_2_0.xsd"
  version="2.0">
    
  <description>JSTL 1.1 functions library</description>
  <display-name>JSTL functions</display-name>
  <tlib-version>1.1</tlib-version>
  <short-name>fn</short-name>
  <uri>http://java.sun.com/jsp/jstl/functions</uri>

  <function>
    <description>
      Tests if an input string contains the specified substring.
    </description>
    <name>contains</name>
    <function-class>org.apache.taglibs.standard.functions.Functions</function-class>
    <function-signature>boolean contains(java.lang.String, java.lang.String)</function-signature>
    <example>
      &lt;c:if test="${fn:contains(name, searchString)}">
    </example>
  </function>

  <function>
    <description>
      Tests if an input string contains the specified substring in a case insensitive way.
    </description>
    <name>containsIgnoreCase</name>
    <function-class>org.apache.taglibs.standard.functions.Functions</function-class>
    <function-signature>boolean containsIgnoreCase(java.lang.String, java.lang.String)</function-signature>
    <example>
      &lt;c:if test="${fn:containsIgnoreCase(name, searchString)}">
    </example>
  </function>

  <function>
    <description>
      Tests if an input string ends with the specified suffix.
    </description>
    <name>endsWith</name>
    <function-class>org.apache.taglibs.standard.functions.Functions</function-class>
    <function-signature>boolean endsWith(java.lang.String, java.lang.String)</function-signature>
    <example>
      &lt;c:if test="${fn:endsWith(filename, ".txt")}">
    </example>
  </function>

  <function>
    <description>
      Escapes characters that could be interpreted as XML markup.
    </description>
    <name>escapeXml</name>

    <function-signature>java.lang.String escapeXml(java.lang.String)</function-signature>
    <example>
      ${fn:escapeXml(param:info)}
    </example>
  </function>

  <function>
    <description>
      Returns the index withing a string of the first occurrence of a specified substring.
    </description>
    <name>indexOf</name>
    <function-class>org.apache.taglibs.standard.functions.Functions</function-class>
    <function-signature>int indexOf(java.lang.String, java.lang.String)</function-signature>
    <example>

    </example>
  </function>

  <function>

    <example>

  <function>
